     416:     function receiptExtractTimeText(value) {
     417:       const text = String(value === null || value === undefined ? "" : value)
     418:         .replace(/：/g, ":")
     419:         .replace(/．/g, ".");
     420: 
     421:       if (!text.trim()) return "";
     422: 
     423:       const patterns = [
     424:         /(^|[^\d])([01]?\d|2[0-3])\s*:\s*([0-5]\d)(?!\d)/,
     425:         /(^|[^\d])([01]?\d|2[0-3])\s*時\s*([0-5]?\d)\s*分?/,
     426:         /(^|[^\d])([01]?\d|2[0-3])\s*\.\s*([0-5]\d)(?!\d)/
     427:       ];
     428: 
     429:       for (const pattern of patterns) {
     430:         const match = text.match(pattern);
     431:         if (!match) continue;
     432: 
     433:         const hour = Number(match[2]);
     434:         const minute = Number(match[3]);
     435: 
     436:         if (
     437:           Number.isFinite(hour) &&
     438:           Number.isFinite(minute) &&
     439:           hour >= 0 &&
     440:           hour <= 23 &&
     441:           minute >= 0 &&
     442:           minute <= 59
     443:         ) {
     444:           return String(hour).padStart(2, "0") + ":" + String(minute).padStart(2, "0");
     445:         }
     446:       }
     447: 
     448:       return "";
     449:     }

     284:     function numValue(value) {
     285:       if (value === null || value === undefined || value === "") return "";
     286: 
     287:       let s = String(value).trim().replace(/,/g, "");
     288:       if (!s) return "";
     289: 
     290:       const n = Number(s);
     291:       if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return String(value);
     292: 
     293:       if (s.indexOf(".") >= 0) {
     294:         s = s.replace(/\.0+$/, "");
     295:         s = s.replace(/(\.\d*?[1-9])0+$/, "$1");
     296:       }
     297: 
     298:       return s;
     299:     }

    1404:                 continue;
    1405:               }
    1406: 
    1407:               draftId = draft.id;
    1408:               payload = buildDraftPayloadForBulk(draft);
    1409:             }
    1410: 
    1411:             await patchDraftForBulk(draftId, payload);
    1412:             success++;
    1413:           } catch (error) {
    1414:             failed++;
    1415:             failedIds.push(id);
    1416:             console.error("まとめて保存失敗 ID " + id, error);
    1417:           }
    1418:         }
    1419:       } finally {
    1420:         if (button) {
    1421:           button.textContent = originalText || "まとめて保存";
    1422:         }
    1423: 
    1424:         setBulkButtonsDisabled(false);
    1425:       }
    1426: 
    1427:       if (selectedId) {
    1428:         await loadDetail(selectedId);
    1429:       } else {
    1430:         await loadList();
    1431:       }
    1432: 
    1433:       alert(
    1434:         "まとめて保存完了\n" +
    1435:         "成功: " + success + " 件\n" +
    1436:         "AI候補なし: " + noDraft + " 件\n" +
    1437:         "失敗: " + failed + " 件" +
    1438:         (failedIds.length ? "\n失敗ID: " + failedIds.join(", ") : "")
    1439:       );
    1440:     }
